 ' Votes were cast in the seventh phase of the Rajmahal Lok Sabha seat of Jharkhand on Sunday (may 19)
 is charan main rajmahal samet 8 rajyon kii 59 loksabhaa siton par voting hui
 a total of 14 candidates are contesting from Rajmahal Lok Sabha seat
 chunaav ayog ne shantipurna tareeke se matdaan sampann karaane ke liye suraksha ke pukhta bandobast kiye hai
 The Rajmahal parliamentary seat was strongly voted and 71
 83% matdaan hua
 By the way, overall 71 in Jharkhand till 5 pm
 16% fisadi voting hui
 As part of the seventh and final phase of the Lok Sabha elections, on Sunday (may 19), 59 seats in 8 states (7 states and 1 union territory) are being held
 jharkhand ke rajmahal sansadeey seat par aaj hi vot daale ja rahe hai
 13 till 9 pm on 3 parliamentary seats of Jharkhand
 19% matdaan ho chukaa he
 On the Rajmahal Lok Sabha seat, the Communist Party of India (marxist), Gopin Soren, Bahujan Samaj Party, Baidnath Pahadia, Trinamool Congress Monika Kisku, Jharkhand Mukti Morcha, Vijay Kumar Hansdak, Bharatiya Janata Party's Hemlal Murmu, All India Forward Bloc, Neeraj Hembrom , Hindustan Nirman Dal has fielded Mahasya Tudu and Bahujan Mukti Party has fielded Mary Nisha Hansdak
 rajmahal loksabhaa seat par 23 may ko voton kii ginati hogi or phir ummidavaaron ke bhagya kaa faisla hoga
 The Rajmahal Lok Sabha seat is spread over Sahibganj and Pakur districts
 yah seat anusuchit janajati ke liye arakshit he
 The area is surrounded by the Rajmahal hills and the Ganges River
 is seat se jharkhand mukti morcha ke vijay kumaar hansadak saansad hai
 Jharkhand has a total of 14 Lok Sabha seats
 madhya kaal main is kshetra ko ugmahal ke naam se janaa jaataa tha
 The area houses the Akbar Mosque and the palace of Nawab Mir Qasim of Bengal
 is seat par bangladeshi ghuspaith sabase ahm mudda he
 It is said that about lakhs of Bangladeshis have taken shelter in Barharwa and Radhanagar police station area of sahibganj district under Rajmahal Lok Sabha constituency
 is seat par saatven charan main matdaan hoga
 Political background Paika Murmu won on the Congress ticket from this seat in 1957
 iske baad congress ke hi tikat par 1962, 1967 or 1971 kaa chunaav ishvar marandi jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 Janata Party's Anton Murmu won from this seat in 1977
 1980 main congress ne phir vaapasi kii or uske tikat par 1980 va 1984 kaa chunaav seth hembhram jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 For the first time in 1989, Jharkhand Mukti Morcha's Kula won this seat and Simon Marandi won the elections of 1989 and 1991 on his ticket
 1996 main congress ke thomas hansda jite
 For the first time in 1998, Kamal played on this seat and won Marandi in Mon on his ticket from here
 1999 main congress ke thomas hansda jite
 Hemlal Murmu of JMM won the 2004 elections
 2009 kaa chunaav bijepi ke devidhan besara jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 jmm's Vijay Kumar Hansdak won the 2014 election
 saamaajit tanabanise loksabhaa seat ke antargat chah vidhansabha siten (rajmahal, borio, barhet, litipaara, pakhud, maheshpur) aate hai
 Of this, Borio, Barhet, Litipara and Maheshpur are reserved for Scheduled Tribes
 2014 ke aam chunaav ke dauraan is seat par matadaataaon kii sankhya kareeb 13

 isamen 6

 is hamale main 166 logon kii maut hui thi
